var
flyingnotebrOK=false;
var
mie=false;
var
aver=parseInt(navigator.appVersion.substring(0,1));
var
aname=navigator.appName;
var
flyingnotemystop=0;
function
flyingnotecheckbrOK()
{ if(aname.indexOf("Internet Explorer")!=-1) { if(aver>=4) flyingnotebrOK=navigator.javaEnabled(); mie=true; }
if(aname.indexOf("Netscape")!=-1)
{ if(aver>=4)
flyingnotebrOK=navigator.javaEnabled();
}
}
var
vmin=2;
var
vmax=5;
var
vr=2;
var
timer1;
function
flyingnotechip(chipname,width,height)
{ this.named=chipname; this.vx=vmin+vmax*Math.random(); this.vy=vmin+vmax*Math.random(); this.w=width; this.h=height; this.xx=0; this.yy=0; this.timer1=null; }
function
flyingnotemovechip(chipname)
{ if(flyingnotebrOK && flyingnotemystop==0) { eval("flyingnotechip="+chipname); if(!mie) { pageX=window.pageXOffset; //pageW=window.innerWidth; pageW=300 pageY=window.pageYOffset; //pageH=window.innerHeight; pageH=250; } else { pageX=window.document.body.scrollLeft; //pageW=window.document.body.offsetWidth-18; pageW=300 pageY=window.document.body.scrollTop; //pageH=window.document.body.offsetHeight; pageH=250; } flyingnotechip.xx=flyingnotechip.xx+flyingnotechip.vx; flyingnotechip.yy=flyingnotechip.yy+flyingnotechip.vy; flyingnotechip.vx+=vr*(Math.random()-0.5); flyingnotechip.vy+=vr*(Math.random()-0.5); if(flyingnotechip.vx>(vmax+vmin)) flyingnotechip.vx=(vmax+vmin)*2-flyingnotechip.vx; if(flyingnotechip.vx<(-vmax-vmin)) flyingnotechip.vx=(-vmax-vmin)*2-flyingnotechip.vx; if(flyingnotechip.vy>(vmax+vmin)) flyingnotechip.vy=(vmax+vmin)*2-flyingnotechip.vy; if(flyingnotechip.vy<(-vmax-vmin)) flyingnotechip.vy=(-vmax-vmin)*2-flyingnotechip.vy; if(flyingnotechip.xx<=pageX) { flyingnotechip.xx=pageX; flyingnotechip.vx=vmin+vmax*Math.random(); } if(flyingnotechip.xx>=pageX+pageW-flyingnotechip.w) { flyingnotechip.xx=pageX+pageW-flyingnotechip.w; flyingnotechip.vx=-vmin-vmax*Math.random(); } if(flyingnotechip.yy<=pageY) { flyingnotechip.yy=pageY; flyingnotechip.vy=vmin+vmax*Math.random(); } if(flyingnotechip.yy>=pageY+pageH-flyingnotechip.h) { flyingnotechip.yy=pageY+pageH-flyingnotechip.h; flyingnotechip.vy=-vmin-vmax*Math.random(); } if(!mie) { eval('document.'+flyingnotechip.named+'.top ='+flyingnotechip.yy); eval('document.'+flyingnotechip.named+'.left='+flyingnotechip.xx); } else { eval('document.all.'+flyingnotechip.named+'.style.pixelLeft='+flyingnotechip.xx); eval('document.all.'+flyingnotechip.named+'.style.pixelTop ='+flyingnotechip.yy); } flyingnotechip.timer1=setTimeout("flyingnotemovechip('"+flyingnotechip.named+"')",200); } }
function
flyingnotestop(x)
{ flyingnotebrOK=true; flyingnotemystop=x; flyingnotemovechip("flyingnotetome"); }
var
flyingnotetome;
var
flyingnotechip;
function
flyingnotetome()
{ flyingnotecheckbrOK(); flyingnotetome=new flyingnotechip("flyingnotetome",180,180); if(flyingnotebrOK) {flyingnotemovechip("flyingnotetome");} }
ns4=(document.layers)?true:false;
ie4=(document.all)?true:false;
function
flyingnoteover()
{ if(ns4){ eval('document.flyingnote.left=document.'+flyingnotechip.named+'.left'); eval('document.flyingnote.top=document.'+flyingnotechip.named+'.top-15'); document.flyingnote.visibility="show"; } else if(ie4){ document.all.flyingnote.style.left=parseInt(document.all.flyingnotetome.style.left); document.all.flyingnote.style.top=parseInt(document.all.flyingnotetome.style.top); document.all.flyingnote.style.visibility="visible"; flyingnotestop(1); } }
function
flyingnoteout()
{ if(ns4){document.flyingnote.visibility="hide";} else if(ie4){ document.all.flyingnote.style.visibility="hidden"; flyingnotestop(0); } }
